$(function(){
//当鼠标滑动到诚信房源专区tab上时，判断气泡是否存在，不存在就显示下拉描述
	$('#chengxin').hover(function(){

	},function(e){

//诚信信息列表标题后的盾牌
	$('.dun').hover(function(){
		var currenttag = $(this);
		currenttag.parent(".fang-list-pos").css("z-index","1");
		var offset = currenttag.offset(); 
		var controltag = $(this).siblings(".cx-icon-tc");
		var parenttag = $(this).parent();
		var parentoffset = parenttag.offset();
		controltag.css("position","absolute");
		controltag.css("top",offset.top-parentoffset.top+27+'px');
		controltag.css("left",offset.left-parentoffset.left-8+'px');
		controltag.show();
		//$(this).parent().children(".cx-icon-tc").show();
	},function(){
		$(this).parent(".fang-list-pos").css("z-index","");
		$(this).siblings(".cx-icon-tc").hide();
	});
});

	//住哪 
	var cityListName = 'bj' ;
	var cateListName = 'zufang' ;
	var cityCNName = '北京';
	function fissionStyle(){
		
		var fissionObj = $('#list-fission-new-id') ;
		if(fissionObj.css('display')=='none'){
			var redirect = new Array() ;
			redirect.push(window.location.protocol);
			redirect.push("//");
			redirect.push(window.location.hostname);
			redirect.push("/");
			redirect.push(cateListName);
			redirect.push("/");
			redirect.push("?lbtabshow=1");
			redirect = redirect.join("") ;
			window.location.href = redirect;
			return false ;
		}else{
			var httpUrl = window.location.href ;
			if(httpUrl.indexOf("?lbtabshow=1")!=-1||httpUrl.indexOf("&amp;lbtabshow=1")!=-1||httpUrl.indexOf("?specialkey=1")!=-1||httpUrl.indexOf("&amp;specialkey=1")!=-1){
				var redirect = new Array() ;
				redirect.push(window.location.protocol);
				redirect.push("//");
				redirect.push(window.location.hostname);
				redirect.push("/");
				redirect.push(cateListName);
				redirect.push("/");
				var querystring = window.location.search.replace("?lbtabshow=1","").replace("&amp;lbtabshow=1","").replace("?specialkey=1","").replace("&amp;specialkey=1","") ;
				if(querystring.substring(0,1)=='&amp;') querystring = "?"+querystring.substring(1,querystring.length) ;
				redirect.push(querystring);
				window.location.href = redirect.join("");
			}
			fissionObj.hide() ;
			$("#fissionid").removeClass('select');
		}
		clickLog('from=fc_'+cateListName+'_zn_'+cityListName);
	}

	//裂变--通过js来控制是否展开 选中
	var fissionDisplay = function(){
		var httpUrl = window.location.href ;
		var fissionObj = $('#list-fission-new-id') ;
		
		//lbtabshow=1/2
		if(httpUrl.indexOf("lbtabshow")!=-1){
			$("#fissionid").addClass('select');
			fissionObj.show() ;
			var douzhuna = $('#lb-douzhuna') ;
			var pianyiduanzu = $('#lb-pianyiduanzu');
			var douzhunadiv = $('#lb-douzhuna-div');
			var pianyiduanzudiv = $('#lb-pianyiduanzu-div');
			
			if(httpUrl.indexOf("lbtabshow=1")!=-1&amp;&amp;httpUrl.indexOf("lbtabshow=2")!=-1){
				//default
				douzhuna.removeClass("on") ;
				pianyiduanzu.addClass("on") ;
				douzhunadiv.hide() ;
				pianyiduanzudiv.show() ;
			}else if(httpUrl.indexOf("lbtabshow=1")!=-1&amp;&amp;httpUrl.indexOf("lbtabshow=2")==-1){
				//tab1
				var tagArr = window.location.search.match(new RegExp("[\?\&amp;]key=([^\&amp;]*)(\&amp;?)", "i")); 
				var specialkeyArr = window.location.search.match(new RegExp("[\?\&amp;]specialkey=([^\&amp;]*)(\&amp;?)", "i")); 
				if(specialkeyArr!=null&amp;&amp;specialkeyArr!='null'){
					$('.list-fission-a a').each(function(){
	                	if($(this).html() == decodeURI('个人房源')&amp;&amp;httpUrl.indexOf('/zufang/1/')==-1){
	                		$(this).siblings('.on').removeClass('on');
	                		$(this).addClass('on');
	                	}
	                })
				}else{
					$('.list-fission-a a').each(function(){
						if(tagArr!=null&amp;&amp;tagArr.length&gt;0){
		                	if($(this).html() == decodeURI(tagArr[1])||$(this).html() == tagArr[1]){
		                		$(this).siblings('.on').removeClass('on');
		                		$(this).addClass('on');
		                	}
						}
	                })
				}
				douzhuna.removeClass("on") ;
				pianyiduanzu.addClass("on") ;
				douzhunadiv.hide() ;
				pianyiduanzudiv.show() ;
			}else if(httpUrl.indexOf("lbtabshow=1")==-1&amp;&amp;httpUrl.indexOf("lbtabshow=2")!=-1){
				//tab2
				pianyiduanzu.removeClass("on") ;
				douzhuna.addClass("on") ;
				douzhunadiv.show() ;
				pianyiduanzudiv.hide() ;
			}else{
				//default
				douzhuna.removeClass("on") ;
				pianyiduanzu.addClass("on") ;
				douzhunadiv.hide() ;
				pianyiduanzudiv.show() ;
			}
		}else{
			fissionObj.hide() ;
			$("#fissionid").removeClass('select');
		}
		
		//解决选中区域展示的问题
        $('.secitem a').each(function(){
	     	if($(this).hasClass('select')&amp;&amp;($(this).html().indexOf('住哪')==-1&amp;&amp;$(this).html().indexOf('全')==-1&amp;&amp;$(this).html().indexOf('不限')==-1&amp;&amp;$(this).html().indexOf('整套出租')==-1)){
	     		fissionObj.hide() ;
				$("#fissionid").removeClass('select');
	     	}
        })
		
	}
fissionDisplay();
var hrefLog = function(cateName,key,href){
	//统计完日志再跳转
	clickLog("from=fc_"+cateName+"_"+key+"_"+cityListName);
	window.location.href=href ;
}

//附近商圈
var alldt = $("#hotarea dt");
function showNear(dt){
    alldt.each(function(){
        if(this == dt) {$(this).next("dd").show();$(this).addClass("select");}
        else {$(this).next("dd").hide();$(this).removeClass("select");}
    });
}
alldt.each(function(){
    $(this).click(function(){showNear(this);}).hover(function(){showNear(this);});
});
showNear(alldt[0]);
boot.require('dom, anim.hover', function(Frame, dom, hover){
	var cc = dom.get('infolist'),
	    trs = cc.getElementsByTagName('tr');
	Frame.each(trs, function(item){
		hover.bind(item, 'bg');
	});
});
$(".selector").each(function(){
	$(this).hover(function(){$(this).addClass("hover")},function(){$(this).removeClass("hover")});
});

var mutexs = [{searchitem:/b\d+/, params:["minprice"], searthname:'租金'}];
boot.require('util.uri', function(Frame, uri){
for(var i = 0, leni = mutexs.length; i &lt; leni; i ++) {
    var mutex = mutexs[i];
    var pobj = {};
    for(var j = 0, lenj = mutex.params.length; j &lt; lenj; j ++) {
        pobj[mutex.params[j]] = null;
    }
    
    for(var l = 0, lenl = mutex.params.length; l &lt; lenl; l ++) {
        var pitem = $("#selection .secitem dt:contains("+mutex.searthname+")").parent();
        if(window.location.search.indexOf(mutex.params[l]) != -1) {
            pitem.find(".select").removeClass("select");
        }
        
        pitem.find("a").each(function(){
            var o = {};
            o[mutex.params] = null;
            this.href = (new uri(this.href)).setQuery(o);
        });
    }
}
});

var dom_events = {

		fun:function(){_gaq.push(['pageTracker._trackEvent', 'list', 'wenbenzhanshi_btn_click', '/bj/house/zufang/']);}
	}

		fun:function(){_gaq.push(['pageTracker._trackEvent', 'list', 'shangquanzhidan_btn_click', '/bj/house/zufang/']);}
	}
	,'#keyword1':{
		evt:'keyup',
		fun:function(){win1.GetContentData();}
	}

		evt:'mouseover',
		fun:function(){$(this).addClass('hover');}
	}
	,'.sbtn':{
		evt:'mouseout',
		fun:function(){$(this).removeClass('hover');}
	}
	,'#searchsite':{
		fun:b_query_all
	}
	,'#selection .subarea .nearsq input:checkbox':{
		fun:function(){
		    if(!this.checked)return;
		    var sc = $('#selection .subarea .nearsq input:checkbox[checked]');
			var maxsq = 4;  
		    if(sc.length &gt; maxsq) {
		        alert('最多选择'+maxsq+'个商圈。');
		        return false;
		    }
		}
	}
	,'#queryconfirm':{
		fun:function(){
		    boot.require('util.uri', function(Frame, uri){
				var sc = $('#selection .subarea .nearsq input:checkbox[checked]'),
					url = new uri(),
					local = url.path.local;
				if(local) {
					local = local.split('_').slice(0,1);
				} else {
					local = [];
				}
				
				for(var i = 0, leni = sc.length; i &lt; leni; i ++) {
					local.push(sc[i].value);
				}
				url.path.local = local.join('_');
				location.href = url.toString();
			});  
		}
	}
	,'#tosq&gt;.tosqa':{
		fun:function(event){
		    if($("#tosq").hasClass('tosqhover')) $("#tosq").removeClass('tosqhover');
		    else {
		    	$("#tosq").addClass('tosqhover');
		    	$("#areazf dd:gt(0)").hide();
		    	$("#areazf dt").removeClass('select');
		    	$("#areazf dt:eq(0)").addClass('select');
		    }
		    event.stopPropagation();
		}
	}
	,'.prifilter input:text':{
		fun:function(event){
			$('#pricefilter').show();
			$('#pricefilter input:button').bind('click', function(){b_query();});
			event.stopPropagation();
		}
	}
	,'.prifilter input[name="b_q"]':{
		evt:'keyup',
		fun:function(){cknum(this);}
	}
	,'#textshow':{
		fun:function(){g2({selpic:1});return false;}
	}
	,'#ispic':{
		fun:function(){click_Ispic(this);}
	}
			};

		value.evt = 'click';

//发统计
var j4fe = ____json4fe,objCatg,objLocallist;
objCatg = $.isArray(j4fe.catentry)?j4fe.catentry[j4fe.catentry.length-1]:j4fe.catentry;
objLocallist = $.isArray(j4fe.locallist)?j4fe.locallist[0]:j4fe.locallist;
var catgName = objCatg.listname || '',cityName = objLocallist.listname || '';
window.stat_params={
	isAuth:-1,
	catgName:catgName,
	cityName:cityName,
	business:'fc',
	pageType:'list'
};
window.sendStat = function (conf) {
	var obj = $.extend({}, conf);
	var fe = window.parent.____json4fe;
	var LoginUid = '';
	var uid = document.cookie.match(/UID=(\d+)/);
	if (uid &amp;&amp; uid.length) {
		LoginUid = uid[1];
	}
	obj['LoginUid'] = LoginUid;
	obj['tel'] = '';
	obj['is_biz'] = fe.isbiz || false;
	obj['AreaPath'] = '';
	if (fe.locallist &amp;&amp; fe.locallist.length) {
		var ids = [];
		for (var i = 0; i &lt; fe.locallist.length; i++) {
			ids[i] = fe.locallist[i]['dispid'];
		}
		obj['AreaPath'] = ids.join(',');
	}
	obj['CatePath'] = '';
	
	if (fe.catentry &amp;&amp; fe.catentry.length) {
		var cates = [];
		for (var i = 0; i &lt; fe.catentry.length; i++) {
			cates[i] = fe.catentry[i]['dispid'];
		}
		obj['CatePath'] = cates.join(',');
	}
	obj['infoid'] = fe.infoid || '';
	obj['userid'] = fe.userid || '';
	obj['infoStat'] = '';
	obj['refUrl'] = escape(window.parent.document.referrer || '');
	obj['Url'] = escape(window.parent.location.href);

	var str = [];
	for (var o in obj) {
		str.push(o + '=' + obj[o]);
	}
	(typeof clickLog === 'function') &amp;&amp; clickLog(str.join('&amp;'));
}

		var that=this;

		},100)
});

	clearTimeout(timeout);
	$(this).show();
}).mouseleave(function(){
	$(this).hide();
});
